Customers\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            whatsapp_id TEXT UNIQUE,\n            name TEXT,\n            email TEXT,\n            registered_at TEXT\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    # Bookings\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            customer_id INTEGER,\n            service TEXT,\n            datetime TEXT,\n            status TEXT,\n            created_at TEXT,\n            FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ninit_db()\n\n# --- Helper Functions ---\ndef get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"SELECT * FROM customers WHERE whatsapp_id=?\", (whatsapp_id,))\n    customer = c.fetchone()\n    conn.close()\n    return customer\n\ndef register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO customers (whatsapp_id, name, email, registered_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\",\n              (whatsapp_id, name, email, datetime.utcnow().isoformat()))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_booking(customer_id, service, dt):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, datetime, status, created_at)\n        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    \"\"\", (customer_id, service, dt, \"pending\", datetime.utcnow().isoformat()))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_bookings():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT b.id, c.name, c.whatsapp_id, b.service, b.datetime, b.status\n        FROM bookings b\n        JOIN customers c ON b.customer_id = c.id\n        ORDER BY b.created_at DESC\n    \"\"\")\n    bookings = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return bookings\n\ndef update_booking_status(booking_id, status):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"UPDATE bookings SET status=? Optionally use user_id for personalization/context\n    response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n        model=\"gpt-3.5-turbo\",\n        messages=[{\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are a helpful assistant for a service business.\"},\n                  {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}]\n    )\n    return response.choices[0].message['content']\n\n# --- WhatsApp Webhook Endpoint ---\n@app.route(\"/webhook\", methods=[\"POST\"])\ndef whatsapp_webhook():\n    data = request.get_json()\n    # Meta Cloud API webhook structure\n    try:\n        entry = data['entry'][0]\n        changes = entry['changes'][0]\n        value = changes['value']\n        messages = value.get('messages', [])\n        for msg in messages:\n            whatsapp_id = msg['from']\n            text = msg['text']['body'].strip() if 'text' in msg else \"\"\n            customer = get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id)\n            if not customer:\n                # Registration flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"register\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Register Name Email\"\n                    parts = text.split()\n                    if len(parts) >= 3:\n                        name = parts[1]\n                        email = parts[2]\n                        register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email)\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Thank you {name}, you are registered!\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To register, send: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n                else:\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Welcome! Please register by sending: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n            else:\n                # Booking flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"book\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\"\n                    parts = text.split(maxsplit=3)\n                    if len(parts) == 4:\n                        service = parts[1]\n                        dt = parts[2] + \" \" + parts[3]\n                        try:\n                            datetime.strptime(dt, \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M\")\n                            create_booking(customer[0], service, dt)\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Booking received for {service} on {dt}. We'll confirm soon.\")\n                        except ValueError:\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Invalid date/time format. Use: Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To book, send: Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n                elif text.lower() == \"my bookings\":\n                    # List bookings\n                    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n                    c = conn.cursor()\n                    c.execute(\"SELECT service, datetime, status FROM bookings WHERE customer_id=?\", (customer[0],))\n                    bookings = c.fetchall()\n                    conn.close()\n                    if bookings:\n                        msg = \"\\n\".join([f\"{b[0]} on {b[1]} - {b[2]}\" for b in bookings])\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Your bookings:\\n\" + msg)\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"You have no bookings.\")\n                else:\n                    # ChatGPT fallback\n                    reply = chatgpt_response(text, whatsapp_id)\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, reply)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(\"Error in webhook:\", e)\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"received\"})\n\n# --- Admin Dashboard ---\n@app.route(\"/admin\", methods=[\"GET\", \"POST\"])\ndef admin_login():\n    if request.method == \"POST\":\n        pwd = request.form.get(\"password\")\n        if pwd == ADMIN_PASSWORD:\n            session['admin'] = True\n            return redirect(url_for(\"admin_dashboard\"))\n        else:\n            return render_template_string(ADMIN_LOGIN_TEMPLATE, error=\"Invalid password\")\n    return render_template_string(ADMIN_LOGIN_TEMPLATE)\n\n@app.route(\"/admin/dashboard\")\ndef admin_dashboard():\n    if not session.get('admin'):\n        return redirect(url_for(\"admin_login\"))\n    bookings = get_bookings()\n    return render_template_string(ADMIN_DASHBOARD_TEMPLATE, bookings=bookings)\n\n@app.route(\"/admin/booking/<int:booking_id>/<status>\")\ndef admin_update_booking(booking_id, status):\n    if not session.get('admin'):\n        return redirect(url_for(\"admin_login\"))\n    update_booking_status(booking_id, status)\n    # Bookings\n    c.execute('''\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            customer_id INTEGER,\n            service TEXT,\n            date TEXT,\n            status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',\n            FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)\n        )\n    ''')\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ninit_db()\n\n# --- Helper Functions ---\ndef db_conn():\n    return sqlite3.connect(DATABASE)\n\ndef get_customer(wa_number):\n    conn = db_conn()\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"SELECT * FROM customers WHERE wa_number=?\", (wa_number,))\n    customer = c.fetchone()\n    conn.close()\n    return customer\n\ndef register_customer(wa_number, name):\n    conn = db_conn()\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO customers (wa_number, name, registered) VALUES (?, ?, 1)\", (wa_number, name))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_booking(wa_number, service, date):\n    customer = get_customer(wa_number)\n    if not customer:\n        return None\n    customer_id = customer[0]\n    conn = db_conn()\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, date) VALUES (?, ?, ?)\", (customer_id, service, date))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n    return True\n\ndef get_bookings():\n    conn = db_conn()\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT b.id, c.name, c.wa_number, b.service, b.date, b.status\n        FROM bookings b\n        JOIN customers c ON b.customer_id = c.id\n        ORDER BY b.date DESC\n    \"\"\")\n    bookings = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return bookings\n\ndef update_booking_status(booking_id, status):\n    conn = db_conn()\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"UPDATE bookings SET status=? Meta Cloud API webhook format\n    try:\n        wa_number = data['entry'][0]['changes'][0]['value']['messages'][0]['from']\n        wa_text = data['entry'][0]['changes'][0]['value']['messages'][0]['text']['body'].strip()\n    except Exception:\n        return jsonify({\"status\": \"ignored\"}), 200\n\n    customer = get_customer(wa_number)\n\n    # Registration flow\n    if not customer or not customer[3]:\n        if wa_text.lower().startswith(\"register\"):\n            name = wa_text[8:].strip() or \"Customer\"\n            register_customer(wa_number, name)\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, f\"Thank you {name}, you are now registered!\")\n            return jsonify({\"status\": \"registered\"}), 200\n        else:\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, \"Welcome! Please register by sending: Register Your Name\")\n            return jsonify({\"status\": \"awaiting_registration\"}), 200\n\n    # Booking flow\n    if wa_text.lower().startswith(\"book\"):\n        parts = wa_text.split()\n        if len(parts) >= 3:\n            service = parts[1]\n            date = parts[2]\n            create_booking(wa_number, service, date)\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, f\"Your booking for {service} on {date} has been received!\")\n            # Notify admin\n            send_whatsapp_message(ADMIN_PHONE, f\"New booking: {customer[2]} ({wa_number}) booked {service} on {date}\")\n            return jsonify({\"status\": \"booked\"}), 200\n        else:\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, \"To book a service, send: Book [Service] [Date]\")\n            return jsonify({\"status\": \"booking_format_error\"}), 200\n\n    # Admin commands\n    if wa_number == ADMIN_PHONE:\n        if wa_text.lower().startswith(\"approve\"):\n            booking_id = int(wa_text.split()[1])\n            update_booking_status(booking_id, \"approved\")\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, f\"Booking {booking_id} approved.\")\n            # Notify customer\n            conn = db_conn()\n            c = conn.cursor()\n            c.execute(\"SELECT c.wa_number FROM bookings b JOIN customers c ON b.customer_id = c.id WHERE b.id=?\", (booking_id,))\n            customer_wa = c.fetchone()\n            conn.close()\n            if customer_wa:\n                send_whatsapp_message(customer_wa[0], f\"Your booking #{booking_id} has been approved!\")\n            return jsonify({\"status\": \"approved\"}), 200\n        elif wa_text.lower().startswith(\"reject\"):\n            booking_id = int(wa_text.split()[1])\n            update_booking_status(booking_id, \"rejected\")\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, f\"Booking {booking_id} rejected.\")\n            # Notify customer\n            conn = db_conn()\n            c = conn.cursor()\n            c.execute(\"SELECT c.wa_number FROM bookings b JOIN customers c ON b.customer_id = c.id WHERE b.id=?\", (booking_id,))\n            customer_wa = c.fetchone()\n            conn.close()\n            if customer_wa:\n                send_whatsapp_message(customer_wa[0], f\"Your booking #{booking_id} has been rejected.\")\n            return jsonify({\"status\": \"rejected\"}), 200\n\n    # ChatGPT fallback for other queries\n    response = chatgpt_response(wa_text)\n    send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, response)\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"chatgpt\"}), 200\n\n# --- Admin Dashboard ---\n@app.route('/admin')\ndef admin_dashboard():\n    bookings = get_bookings()\n    # Simple HTML dashboard\n    html = \"\"\"\n    <h2>Admin Dashboard - Bookings</h2>\n    <table border=\"1\">\n        <tr>\n            <th>ID</th><th>Name</th><th>WhatsApp</th><th>Service</th><th>Date</th><th>Status</th>\n        </tr>\n        {% for b in bookings %}\n        <tr>\n            <td>{{b[0]}}</td>\n            <td>{{b[1]}}</td>\n            <td>{{b[2]}}</td>\n            <td>{{b[3]}}</td>\n            <td>{{b[4]}}</td>\n            <td>{{b[5]}}</td>\n        </tr>\n        {% endfor %}\n    </table>\n    <p>To approve/reject bookings, send \"Approve [ID]\" or \"Reject [ID]\" via WhatsApp.</p>\n    \"\"\"\n    return render_template_string(html, bookings=bookings)\n\n# --- Health Check ---\n@app.route('/')\ndef index():\n    return \"WhatsApp Chatbot is running!\"\n\n# --- Flask App Entry Point ---\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    # Customers table\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            wa_number TEXT UNIQUE,\n            name TEXT,\n            email TEXT\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    # Bookings table\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            customer_id INTEGER,\n            service TEXT,\n            date TEXT,\n            status TEXT,\n            FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ninit_db()\n\n# --- Helper Functions ---\n\ndef send_whatsapp_message(to_number, message):\n    \"\"\"Send message via Meta WhatsApp Cloud API.\"\"\"\n    headers = {\n        \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {META_TOKEN}\",\n        \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"\n    }\n    data = {\n        \"messaging_product\": \"whatsapp\",\n        \"to\": to_number,\n        \"type\": \"text\",\n        \"text\": {\"body\": message}\n    }\n    response = requests.post(META_API_URL, headers=headers, json=data)\n    return response.ok\n\ndef chatgpt_response(prompt):\n    \"\"\"Get response from OpenAI ChatGPT.\"\"\"\n    response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n        model=\"gpt-3.5-turbo\",\n        messages=[{\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}],\n        max_tokens=150\n    )\n    return response.choices[0].message['content'].strip()\n\ndef get_or_create_customer(wa_number):\n    \"\"\"Fetch or create customer record.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"SELECT * FROM customers WHERE wa_number=?\", (wa_number,))\n    customer = c.fetchone()\n    if customer:\n        conn.close()\n        return customer\n    else:\n        # New customer, ask for registration\n        conn.close()\n        return None\n\ndef register_customer(wa_number, name, email):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO customers (wa_number, name, email) VALUES (?, ?, ?)\", (wa_number, name, email))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_booking(customer_id, service, date):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, date, status) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\",\n              (customer_id, service, date, \"Pending\"))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_bookings():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT bookings.id, customers.name, customers.wa_number, bookings.service, bookings.date, bookings.status\n        FROM bookings\n        JOIN customers ON bookings.customer_id = customers.id\n        ORDER BY bookings.date DESC\n    \"\"\")\n    bookings = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return bookings\n\ndef update_booking_status(booking_id, status):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"UPDATE bookings SET status=? WHERE id=?\", (status, booking_id))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_customer_by_wa(wa_number):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"SELECT * FROM customers WHERE wa_number=?\", (wa_number,))\n    customer = c.fetchone()\n    conn.close()\n    return customer\n\n# --- Flask Routes ---\n\n@app.route('/webhook', methods=['POST'])\ndef webhook():\n    \"\"\"\n    WhatsApp webhook endpoint.\n    Handles incoming messages and responds accordingly.\n    \"\"\"\n    data = request.get_json()\n    print(\"Received webhook:\", data)\n    try:\n        wa_entry = data['entry'][0]['changes'][0]['value']\n        wa_number = wa_entry['messages'][0]['from']\n        wa_text = wa_entry['messages'][0]['text']['body'].strip()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(\"Webhook parse error:\", e)\n        return \"OK\", 200\n\n    customer = get_or_create_customer(wa_number)\n\n    # Registration flow\n    if not customer:\n        if wa_text.lower().startswith(\"register:\"):\n            # Expected format: Register: Name, Email\n            try:\n                _, info = wa_text.split(\":\", 1)\n                name, email = [x.strip() for x in info.split(\",\")]\n                register_customer(wa_number, name, email)\n                send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, f\"Registration successful! Welcome, {name}.\")\n            except Exception:\n                send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, \"Invalid format. Please send:\\nRegister: Your Name, Your Email\")\n        else:\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, \"Welcome! Please register first by sending:\\nRegister: Your Name, Your Email\")\n        return \"OK\", 200\n\n    # Booking flow\n    if wa_text.lower().startswith(\"book:\"):\n        # Expected format: Book: Service, Date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n        try:\n            _, info = wa_text.split(\":\", 1)\n            service, date = [x.strip() for x in info.split(\",\")]\n            create_booking(customer[0], service, date)\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, f\"Booking for '{service}' on {date} received. We'll confirm soon.\")\n            # Notify admin (could be a list of admin numbers)\n            send_whatsapp_message(\"ADMIN_WHATSAPP_NUMBER\", f\"New booking: {customer[1]} ({wa_number}) - {service} on {date}\")\n        except Exception:\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, \"Invalid format. Please send:\\nBook: Service Name, Date (YYYY-MM-DD)\")\n        return \"OK\", 200\n\n    # Status check\n    if wa_text.lower().startswith(\"status\"):\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n        c = conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"\"\"\n            SELECT service, date, status FROM bookings\n            WHERE customer_id=?\n            ORDER BY date DESC\n        \"\"\", (customer[0],))\n        bookings = c.fetchall()\n        conn.close()\n        if bookings:\n            msg = \"Your bookings:\\n\"\n            for b in bookings:\n                msg += f\"- {b[0]} on {b[1]}: {b[2]}\\n\"\n        else:\n            msg = \"You have no bookings yet.\"\n        send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, msg)\n        return \"OK\", 200\n\n    # ChatGPT fallback\n    reply = chatgpt_response(wa_text)\n    send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, reply)\n    return \"OK\", 200\n\n# --- Admin Dashboard ---\n\n@app.route('/admin', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef admin_dashboard():\n    # Notify customer\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n        c = conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"\"\"\n            SELECT customers.wa_number, bookings.service, bookings.date\n            FROM bookings\n            JOIN customers ON bookings.customer_id = customers.id\n            WHERE bookings.id=?\n        \"\"\", (booking_id,))\n        result = c.fetchone()\n        conn.close()\n        if result:\n            wa_number, service, date = result\n            send_whatsapp_message(wa_number, f\"Your booking for '{service}' on {date} is now '{new_status}'.\")\n    bookings = get_bookings()\n    # Meta Cloud API webhook structure\n    try:\n        entry = data['entry'][0]\n        changes = entry['changes'][0]\n        value = changes['value']\n        messages = value.get('messages', [])\n        for msg in messages:\n            whatsapp_id = msg['from']\n            text = msg['text']['body'].strip() if 'text' in msg else \"\"\n            customer = get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id)\n            if not customer:\n                # Registration flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"register\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Register Name Email\"\n                    parts = text.split()\n                    if len(parts) >= 3:\n                        name = parts[1]\n                        email = parts[2]\n                        register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email)\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Thank you {name}, you are registered!\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To register, send: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n                else:\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Welcome! Please register by sending: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n            else:\n                # Booking flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"book\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\"\n                    parts = text.split(maxsplit=3)\n                    if len(parts) == 4:\n                        service = parts[1]\n                        dt = parts[2] + \" \" + parts[3]\n                        try:\n                            datetime.strptime(dt, \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M\")\n                            create_booking(customer[0], service, dt)\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Booking received for {service} on {dt}.        </td>\n    </tr>\n    {% endfor %}\n</table>\n<br>\n<a href=\"{{ url_for('admin_logout') }}\">Logout</a>\n</body>\n</html>\n\"\"\"\n\n# --- WhatsApp Webhook Verification (GET)                         "\"\"\"\nWhatsApp Chatbot with Meta Cloud API, OpenAI ChatGPT Integration,\nCustomer Registration, Service Booking, Admin Dashboard, Notifications,\nBacked by SQLite Database, init_db():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            whatsapp_id TEXT UNIQUE,\n            name TEXT,\n            email TEXT,\n            registered_at TEXT\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings           FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ninit_db()\n\n# --- Helper Functions ---\n\ndef get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"SELECT * FROM customers WHERE whatsapp_id=?\", (whatsapp_id,))\n    customer = c.fetchone()\n    conn.close()\n    return customer\n\ndef register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\n        \"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO customers (whatsapp_id, name, email, registered_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\",\n        (whatsapp_id, name, email, datetime.utcnow().isoformat())\n    )\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_booking(customer_id, service, dt):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, datetime, status, created_at)\n        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    \"\"\", (customer_id, service, dt, \"pending\", datetime.utcnow().isoformat()))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_bookings():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT b.id, c.name, c.whatsapp_id, b.service, b.datetime, b.status\n        FROM bookings b\n        JOIN customers c ON b.customer_id = c.id\n        ORDER BY b.created_at DESC\n    \"\"\")\n    bookings = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return bookings\n\ndef update_booking_status(booking_id, status):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"UPDATE bookings SET status=? WHERE id=?\", (status, booking_id))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef send_whatsapp_message(to, text):\n    \"\"\"\n    Sends a WhatsApp message via Meta Cloud API.\n    \"\"\"\n    url = f\"https://graph.facebook.com/v18.0/{META_PHONE_NUMBER_ID}/messages\"\n    headers = {\n        \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {META_TOKEN}\",\n        \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"\n    }\n    payload = {\n        \"messaging_product\": \"whatsapp\",\n        \"to\": to,\n        \"type\": \"text\",\n        \"text\": {\"body\": text}\n    }\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(url, chatgpt_response(prompt, user_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Gets a response from OpenAI ChatGPT for the given prompt.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n            model=\"gpt-3.5-turbo\",\n            messages=[\n                {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are a helpful assistant for a service business.\"},\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n            ]\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message['content']\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"OpenAI error: {e}\")\n        return \"Sorry, I'm having trouble answering right now.\"\n\n# --- WhatsApp Webhook Verification (GET) ---\n@app.route(\"/webhook\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef whatsapp_verify():\n    mode = request.args.get(\"hub.mode\")\n    token = request.args.get(\"hub.verify_token\")\n    challenge = request.args.get(\"hub.challenge\")\n    if mode == \"subscribe\" and token == META_VERIFY_TOKEN:\n        return challenge, 200\n    else:\n        return \"Verification failed\", 403\n\n# --- WhatsApp Webhook Endpoint (POST) ---\n@app.route(\"/webhook\", methods=[\"POST\"])\ndef whatsapp_webhook():\n    data = request.get_json()\n    try:\n        entry = data.get('entry', [])[0]\n        changes = entry.get('changes', [])[0]\n        value = changes.get('value', {})\n        messages = value.get('messages', [])\n        for msg in messages:\n            whatsapp_id = msg.get('from')\n            text = msg.get('text', {}).get('body', '').strip()\n            if not whatsapp_id:\n                continue\n\n            customer = get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id)\n            if not customer:\n                # Registration flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"register\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Register Name Email\"\n                    parts = text.split()\n                    if len(parts) >= 3:\n                        name = parts[1]\n                        email = parts[2]\n                        register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email)\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Thank you {name}, you are registered!\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To register, send: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n                else:\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Welcome! Please register by sending: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n            else:\n                # Booking flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"book\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\"\n                    parts = text.split(maxsplit=3)\n                    if len(parts) == 4:\n                        service = parts[1]\n                        dt = parts[2] + \" \" + parts[3]\n                        try:\n                            datetime.strptime(dt, \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M\")\n                            create_booking(customer[0], service, dt)\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Booking received for {service} on {dt}. We'll confirm soon.\")\n                        except ValueError:\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Invalid date/time format. Use: Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To book, send: Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n                elif text.lower() == \"my bookings\":\n                    # List bookings\n                    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n                    c = conn.cursor()\n                    c.execute(\"SELECT service, datetime, status FROM bookings WHERE customer_id=? ORDER BY created_at DESC\", (customer[0],))\n                    bookings = c.fetchall()\n                    conn.close()\n                    if bookings:\n                        msg = \"\\n\".join([f\"{b[0]} on {b[1]} - {b[2]}\" for b in bookings])\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Your bookings:\\n\" + msg)\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"You have no bookings.\")\n                else:\n                    # ChatGPT fallback\n                    reply = chatgpt_response(text, whatsapp_id)\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, reply)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(\"Error in webhook:\", e)\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"received\"})\n\n# --- Admin Dashboard Templates ---\nADMIN_LOGIN_TEMPLATE = \"\"\"\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html>\n<head><title>Admin Login</title></head>\n<body>\n<h2>Admin Login</h2>\n{% if error %}<p style=\"color:red;\">{{ error }}</p>{% endif %}\n<form method=\"post\">\n    <input type=\"password\" name=\"password\" placeholder=\"Password\" required>\n    <button \"POST\"])\ndef admin_login():\n    if request.method == \"POST\":\n        pwd = request.form.get(\"password\")\n        if pwd == ADMIN_PASSWORD:\n            session['admin'] = True\n c.id\n        WHERE b.id=?\n    \"\"\", (booking_id,))\n    row = c.fetchone()\n    conn.close()\n    if row:\n        whatsapp_id, service, dt = row\n        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, return redirect(url_for(\"admin_login\"))\n\n# --- Main ---\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # For local testing; for HOSTINGER use waitress-serve\n    app.run(host=\"0.0.0.0\", port=5000)",

    messages=[\n                {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are a helpful assistant for a service business.\"},\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n else:\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Welcome!                send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, reply)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(\"Error in webhook:\", e)\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"received\"})\n\n# --- Admin Dashboard dotenv is optional\n\nMETA_TOKEN = os.getenv(\"META_TOKEN\")  # Meta Cloud API Bearer token\nMETA_PHONE_NUMBER_ID = os.getenv(\"META_PHONE_NUMBER_ID\")  # WhatsApp Phone Number ID\nOPENAI_API_KEY = os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\")\nADMIN_PASSWORD = os.getenv(\"ADMIN_PASSWORD\", \"admin123\")  # Change in production\n\nopenai.api_key = OPENAI_API_KEY\n\n# --- Flask App ---\napp = Flask(__name__)\napp.secret_key = os.getenv(\"FLASK_SECRET_KEY\", \"supersecretkey\")  # Change in production\n\nDB_NAME = \"chatbot.db\"\n\n# --- Database Setup ---\ndef init_db():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    # Customers table\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            whatsapp_id TEXT UNIQUE,\n            name TEXT,\n            email TEXT,\n            registered_at TEXT\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    # Bookings table\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            customer_id INTEGER,\n            service TEXT,\n            datetime TEXT,\n            status TEXT,\n            created_at TEXT,\n            FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ninit_db()\n\n# --- Helper Functions ---\ndef get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"SELECT * FROM customers WHERE whatsapp_id=?\", (whatsapp_id,))\n    customer = c.fetchone()\n    conn.close()\n    return customer\n\ndef register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO customers (whatsapp_id, name, email, registered_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\",\n              (whatsapp_id, name, email, datetime.utcnow().isoformat()))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_booking(customer_id, service, dt):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, datetime, status, created_at)\n        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    \"\"\", (customer_id, service, dt, \"pending\", datetime.utcnow().isoformat()))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_bookings():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT b.id, c.name, c.whatsapp_id, b.service, b.datetime, b.status\n        FROM bookings b\n        JOIN customers c ON b.customer_id = c.id\n        ORDER BY b.created_at DESC\n    \"\"\")\n    bookings = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return bookings\n\ndef update_booking_status(booking_id, status):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"UPDATE bookings SET status=? WHERE id=?\", (status, booking_id))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef send_whatsapp_message(to, text):\n    \"\"\"Send a WhatsApp message via Meta Cloud API.\"\"\"\n    url = f\"https://graph.facebook.com/v18.0/{META_PHONE_NUMBER_ID}/messages\"\n    headers = {\n        \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {META_TOKEN}\",\n        \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"\n    }\n    payload = {\n        \"messaging_product\": \"whatsapp\",\n        \"to\": to,\n        \"type\": \"text\",\n        \"text\": {\"body\": text}\n    }\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=10)\n        return resp.json()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error sending WhatsApp message: {e}\")\n        return {}\n\ndef chatgpt_response(prompt, user_id):\n    \"\"\"Get a response from OpenAI ChatGPT API.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n            model=\"gpt-3.5-turbo\",\n            messages=[\n                {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are a helpful assistant for a service business.\"},\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n            ]\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message['content']\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error from OpenAI API: {e}\")\n        return \"Sorry, I'm having trouble answering right now.\"\n\n# --- WhatsApp Webhook Endpoint ---\n@app.route(\"/webhook\", methods=[\"POST\"])\ndef whatsapp_webhook():\n    data = request.get_json()\n    # Meta Cloud API webhook structure\n    try:\n        entry = data['entry'][0]\n        changes = entry['changes'][0]\n        value = changes['value']\n        messages = value.get('messages', [])\n        for msg in messages:\n            whatsapp_id = msg['from']\n            text = msg['text']['body'].strip() if 'text' in msg else \"\"\n            customer = get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id)\n            if not customer:\n                # Registration flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"register\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Register Name Email\"\n                    parts = text.split(maxsplit=2)\n                    if len(parts) == 3:\n                        name = parts[1]\n                        email = parts[2]\n                        register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email)\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Thank you {name}, you are registered!\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To register, send: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n                else:\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Welcome! Please register by sending: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n            else:\n                # Booking flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"book\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\"\n                    parts = text.split(maxsplit=3)\n                    if len(parts) == 4:\n                        service = parts[1]\n                        dt = parts[2] + \" \" + parts[3]\n                        try:\n                            datetime.strptime(dt, \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M\")\n                            create_booking(customer[0], service, dt)\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Booking received for {service} on {dt}. We'll confirm soon.\")\n                        except ValueError:\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Invalid date/time format. Use: Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To book, send: Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n                elif text.lower() == \"my bookings\":\n                    # List bookings\n                    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n                    c = conn.cursor()\n                    c.execute(\"SELECT service, datetime, status FROM bookings WHERE customer_id=? ORDER BY created_at DESC\", (customer[0],))\n                    bookings = c.fetchall()\n                    conn.close()\n                    if bookings:\n                        msg = \"\\n\".join([f\"{b[0]} on {b[1]} - {b[2]}\" for b in bookings])\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Your bookings:\\n\" + msg)\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"You have no bookings.\")\n                else:\n                    # ChatGPT fallback\n                    reply = chatgpt_response(text, whatsapp_id)\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, reply)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(\"Error in webhook:\", e)\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"received\"})\n\n# --- Admin Dashboard       session['admin'] = True\n            return redirect(url_for(\"admin_dashboard\"))\n        else:\n            return render_template_string(ADMIN_LOGIN_TEMPLATE, error=\"Invalid password\")\n          created_at TEXT,\n            FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ninit_db()\n\n# --- Helper Functions ---\ndef get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id):\n    \"\"\"Return customer tuple by WhatsApp ID, or None.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"SELECT * FROM customers WHERE whatsapp_id=?\", (whatsapp_id,))\n    customer = c.fetchone()\n    conn.close()\n    return customer\n\ndef register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email):\n    \"\"\"Register a new customer if not exists.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO customers (whatsapp_id, name, email, registered_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\",\n              (whatsapp_id, name, email, datetime.utcnow().isoformat()))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_booking(customer_id, service, dt):\n    \"\"\"Create a new booking for a customer.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, datetime, status, created_at)\n        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    \"\"\", (customer_id, service, dt, \"pending\", datetime.utcnow().isoformat()))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_bookings():\n    \"\"\"Return all bookings joined with customer info.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT b.id, c.name, c.whatsapp_id, b.service, b.datetime, b.status\n        FROM bookings b\n        JOIN customers c ON b.customer_id = c.id\n        ORDER BY b.created_at DESC\n    \"\"\")\n    bookings = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return bookings\n\ndef Meta Cloud API webhook structure\n    try:\n        entry = data['entry'][0]\n        changes = entry['changes'][0]\n        value = changes['value']\n        messages = value.get('messages', [])\n        for msg in messages:\n            whatsapp_id = msg['from']\n            text = msg['text']['body'].strip() if 'text' in msg else \"\"\n            customer = get_customer_by_whatsapp(whatsapp_id)\n            if not customer:\n                # Registration flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"register\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Register Name Email\"\n                    parts = text.split(maxsplit=2)\n                    if len(parts) == 3:\n                        name = parts[1]\n                        email = parts[2]\n                        register_customer(whatsapp_id, name, email)\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Thank you {name}, you are registered!\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To register, send: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n                else:\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Welcome! Please register by sending: Register YourName YourEmail\")\n            else:\n                # Booking flow\n                if text.lower().startswith(\"book\"):\n                    # Expect: \"Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\"\n                    parts = text.split(maxsplit=3)\n                    if len(parts) == 4:\n                        service = parts[1]\n                        dt = parts[2] + \" \" + parts[3]\n                        try:\n                            datetime.strptime(dt, \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M\")\n                            create_booking(customer[0], service, dt)\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Booking received for {service} on {dt}. We'll confirm soon.\")\n                        except ValueError:\n                            send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Invalid date/time format. Use: Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"To book, send: Book Service YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n                elif text.lower() == \"my bookings\":\n                    # List bookings\n                    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)\n                    c = conn.cursor()\n                    c.execute(\"SELECT service, datetime, status FROM bookings WHERE customer_id=? ORDER BY created_at DESC\", (customer[0],))\n                    bookings = c.fetchall()\n                    conn.close()\n                    if bookings:\n                        msg = \"\\n\".join([f\"{b[0]} on {b[1]} - {b[2]}\" for b in bookings])\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"Your bookings:\\n\" + msg)\n                    else:\n                        send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, \"You have no bookings.\")\n                else:\n                    # ChatGPT fallback for general queries\n                    reply = chatgpt_response(text, whatsapp_id)\n                    send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, reply)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(\"Error in webhook:\", e)\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"received\"})\n\n# --- Admin Dashboard ---\n@app.route(\"/admin\", methods=[\"GET\", \"POST\"])\ndef admin_login():\n    \"\"\"Admin login page.\"\"\"\n    if request.method == \"POST\":\n        pwd send_whatsapp_message(whatsapp_id, f\"Your booking for {service} on {dt} is now {status}.\")\n    return redirect(url_for(\"admin_dashboard\"))\n\n@app.route(\"/admin/logout\")\ndef admin_logout():\n        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            whatsapp_id TEXT UNIQUE,\n            name TEXT,\n            email TEXT,\n            registered_at TEXT\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n        # Use local copy of function\n        def send_whatsapp_message(to, text):\n            url = f\"https://graph.facebook.com/v18.0/{META_PHONE_NUMBER_ID}/messages\"\n            headers = {\n                \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {META_TOKEN}\",\n                \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"\n            }\n            payload = {\n                \"messaging_product\":
